class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Cargo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="font-size:95%"><tbody><tr><th>Airlines</th><th class="unsortable">Destinations</th></tr><tr><td><a href="/wiki/FedEx_Feeder" class="mw-redirect" title="FedEx Feeder">FedEx Feeder</a><sup id="cite_ref-359" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-359">&#91;359&#93;</a></sup> </td><td> <a href="/wiki/Charles_de_Gaulle_Airport" title="Charles de Gaulle Airport">Paris\xe2\x80\x93Charles de Gaulle</a>\n</td></tr><tr><td><a href="/wiki/UPS_Airlines" title="UPS Airlines">UPS Airlines</a><sup id="cite_ref-sprintair_360-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sprintair-360">&#91;360&#93;</a></sup> </td><td> <a href="/wiki/Cologne_Bonn_Airport" title="Cologne Bonn Airport">Cologne/Bonn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gda%C5%84sk_Lech_Wa%C5%82%C4%99sa_Airport" title="Gda\xc5\x84sk Lech Wa\xc5\x82\xc4\x99sa Airport">Gda\xc5\x84sk</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ground_transportation">Ground transportation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Ground transportation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Transport_in_Berlin" title="Transport in Berlin">Transport in Berlin</a></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rail">Rail</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Rail">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg/220px-BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="156" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg/330px-BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg/440px-BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2800" data-file-height="1982" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:BER_Anbindung_2020.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of  bus and rail connections into and around Berlin. An express line serves <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Hauptbahnhof" title="Berlin Hauptbahnhof">Berlin Hauptbahnhof</a> in 30 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-361" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-361">&#91;361&#93;</a></sup></div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg/220px-Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg/330px-Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg/440px-Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6006" data-file-height="4004" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Berlin_brandenburg_airport_station.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Interior of the airport station</div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/BER_Airport_%E2%80%93_Terminal_1-2_station" title="BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 1-2 station">BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 1-2 station</a> and <a href="/wiki/BER_Airport_%E2%80%93_Terminal_5_station" title="BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 5 station">BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 5 station</a></div>\n<p>The terminal connects to a 3.1-kilometre (1.9&#160;mi) east\xe2\x80\x93west railway tunnel under the apron and the terminal complex. As the nine tunnel sections were the first structures to be built, they were constructed by conventional excavations.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/BER_Airport_%E2%80%93_Terminal_1-2_station" title="BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 1-2 station">BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 1-2 station</a> has six tracks and forms the lowest level of Terminal 1\xe2\x80\x932.<sup id="cite_ref-businessonde_362-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-businessonde-362">&#91;362&#93;</a></sup> Two tracks serve as a terminus for the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_S-Bahn" title="Berlin S-Bahn">S-Bahn</a> \xe2\x80\x93 with the <a href="/wiki/S9_(Berlin)" title="S9 (Berlin)">S9</a> serving the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Stadtbahn" title="Berlin Stadtbahn">Stadtbahn</a> and the <a href="/wiki/S45_(Berlin)" title="S45 (Berlin)">S45</a> serving the southern <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Ringbahn" title="Berlin Ringbahn">Ringbahn</a>. The other four tracks handle <a href="/wiki/EuroCity" title="EuroCity">EuroCity</a>, <a href="/wiki/InterCity" title="InterCity">InterCity</a>, <a href="/wiki/Intercity-Express" class="mw-redirect" title="Intercity-Express">Intercity-Express</a> and <a href="/wiki/Regional-Express" title="Regional-Express">Regional-Express</a> trains. The Terminal 5 complex is served by <a href="/wiki/BER_Airport_%E2%80%93_Terminal_5_station" title="BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 5 station">BER Airport \xe2\x80\x93 Terminal 5 station</a> which previously served the former Sch\xc3\xb6nefeld Airport.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Bahn" title="Deutsche Bahn">Deutsche Bahn</a> confirmed in August 2011 that multiple daily Intercity-Express and InterCity trains will connect the airport to <a href="/wiki/Bielefeld" title="Bielefeld">Bielefeld</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hannover" class="mw-redirect" title="Hannover">Hannover</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hamburg" title="Hamburg">Hamburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dresden" title="Dresden">Dresden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leipzig" title="Leipzig">Leipzig</a>, <a href="/wiki/Halle,_Saxony-Anhalt" class="mw-redirect" title="Halle, Saxony-Anhalt">Halle</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wolfsburg" title="Wolfsburg">Wolfsburg</a>. EuroCity trains will also connect to <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Wroc\xc5\x82aw">Wroc\xc5\x82aw</a> and <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Krak\xc3\xb3w">Krak\xc3\xb3w</a> in <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prague" title="Prague">Prague</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_363-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-363">&#91;363&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>About half of the passengers are expected to access BER by rail. An express line (<a href="/wiki/Regionalbahn" title="Regionalbahn">Regionalbahn</a>) will connect the airport with the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Hauptbahnhof" title="Berlin Hauptbahnhof">Berlin Hauptbahnhof</a> (Berlin main station) in 30 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-bahnof_364-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bahnof-364">&#91;364&#93;</a></sup> Two more stops at <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Potsdamer_Platz_station" title="Berlin Potsdamer Platz station">Potsdamer Platz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Berlin_S%C3%BCdkreuz" title="Berlin S\xc3\xbcdkreuz">Berlin S\xc3\xbcdkreuz</a> will be part of the Airport Express, which is planned to make the trip in 20 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_363-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-363">&#91;363&#93;</a></sup> As of 2019, rebuilding the <a href="/wiki/Berlin%E2%80%93Dresden_railway" title="Berlin\xe2\x80\x93Dresden railway">Berlin\xe2\x80\x93Dresden railway</a> that would allow the 20-minute trip to Hauptbahnhof is expected to finish in 2025.<sup id="cite_ref-dresdner-bahn-2019_365-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dresdner-bahn-2019-365">&#91;365&#93;</a></sup> Until then, the express train will run via <a href="/wiki/Berlin-Gesundbrunnen_station" title="Berlin-Gesundbrunnen station">Berlin-Gesundbrunnen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ostkreuz" title="Ostkreuz">Ostkreuz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-366" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-366">&#91;366&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>According to the district administrator of <a href="/wiki/Dahme-Spreewald" title="Dahme-Spreewald">Dahme-Spreewald</a>, train rides from southern Brandenburg towards BER might be complicated and require changing trains. He suggested a new rail concept might be necessary.<sup id="cite_ref-367" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-367">&#91;367&#93;</a></sup> Final construction permission for the railway station was granted on 26 March 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-368" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-368">&#91;368&#93;</a></sup> The final permit for Dresdner Bahn construction was granted on 13 September 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-dresdner-bahn-2019_365-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dresdner-bahn-2019-365">&#91;365&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Proposed_expansions">Proposed expansions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Proposed expansions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<dl><dt>U-Bahn</dt></dl>\n<p><a href="/wiki/U7_(Berlin_U-Bahn)" title="U7 (Berlin U-Bahn)">Line U7</a> terminates short of the airport (at <a href="/wiki/Rudow_(Berlin_U-Bahn)" title="Rudow (Berlin U-Bahn)">Rudow</a>) but there are plans to extend it towards the airport if and when funds become available. The issue is complicated by the fact that the line would have to cross the state border between Berlin and Brandenburg and it is unclear who would have to pay for which parts of construction operations and maintenance. While Berlin has many "ghost stations" built in preparation for potential future construction, there is no provision underneath the terminal building for a station.<sup id="cite_ref-369" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-369">&#91;369&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-370" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-370">&#91;370&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-371" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-371">&#91;371&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-372" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-372">&#91;372&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<dl><dt>Magnetic levitation railway</dt></dl>\n<p>In June 2020, the <a href="/wiki/Christian_Democratic_Union_of_Germany" title="Christian Democratic Union of Germany">CDU</a> Berlin (then in opposition at the state level) proposed building a <a href="/wiki/Magnetic_Levitation_Train" class="mw-redirect" title="Magnetic Levitation Train">Magnetic Levitation Train</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Transport_System_B%C3%B6gl" title="Transport System B\xc3\xb6gl">Transport System B\xc3\xb6gl</a> (developed by the Bavarian construction company <a href="/wiki/Max_B%C3%B6gl" title="Max B\xc3\xb6gl">Max B\xc3\xb6gl</a>) to the airport.<sup id="cite_ref-373" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-373">&#91;373&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-374" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-374">&#91;374&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-375" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-375">&#91;375&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-376" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-376">&#91;376&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-377" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-377">&#91;377&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Road">Road</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Road">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png/220px-Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="159" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png/330px-Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png/440px-Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1085" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Berlin_Stra%C3%9Fenverkehr_BER.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Map of motorways in Berlin</div></div></div>\n<p>Berlin Brandenburg Airport is connected by its own exit to the <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_113" title="Bundesautobahn 113">A113</a>. The road carries traffic into Berlin to the <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_100" title="Bundesautobahn 100">A100</a> and out to the <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_10" title="Bundesautobahn 10">A10</a> where it continues south as the <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_13" title="Bundesautobahn 13">A13</a> in the direction of Dresden. The <a href="/wiki/Bundesstra%C3%9Fe_96" title="Bundesstra\xc3\x9fe 96">highway 96a</a> along the north side of the airport is being expanded to four lanes towards <a href="/wiki/Potsdam" title="Potsdam">Potsdam</a>.\n</p><p>Four car parks and a car rental centre will be completed by the opening of BER. Around 10,000 parking spaces will be available in four <a href="/wiki/Multi-storey_car_park" class="mw-redirect" title="Multi-storey car park">multi-storey car parks</a>.\n</p><p>A study released in September 2016 attested that BER will double the amount of vehicular traffic, causing frequent traffic jams on the <a href="/wiki/Autobahn" title="Autobahn">Autobahn</a> once the airport opens. The A100 and A113 do not have enough lanes to support the expected volume of traffic. The approach to BER was deemed insufficient for the expected traffic and will lead to heavy congestion on the highways throughout south-central Berlin.<sup id="cite_ref-traffic-disaster_378-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-traffic-disaster-378">&#91;378&#93;</a></sup> There are also concerns at increased accidents and air pollution.<sup id="cite_ref-379" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-379">&#91;379&#93;</a></sup>\nCongestion is expected to be high in tunnels leading to the airport, causing frequent closings of the Britz tunnel on the A100.<sup id="cite_ref-380" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-380">&#91;380&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-381" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-381">&#91;381&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-382" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-382">&#91;382&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Over 10% of passengers are expected to come from <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-383" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-383">&#91;383&#93;</a></sup> also thanks to upgraded highways on the Polish side of the border. It is hoped that these upgrades will make the airport accessible for air travellers from the western regions of that country.<sup id="cite_ref-motorway_384-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-motorway-384">&#91;384&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bus">Bus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Bus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Public transport connections at the new airport  include numerous bus services. BER is served by the express buses X7, X71 and X11. The X7 connects to the <a href="/wiki/U7_(Berlin_U-Bahn)" title="U7 (Berlin U-Bahn)">U7</a> subway at <a href="/wiki/Rudow_(Berlin_U-Bahn)" title="Rudow (Berlin U-Bahn)">Rudow station</a>. X71 connects the airport to <a href="/wiki/Alt_Mariendorf_(Berlin_U-Bahn)" class="mw-redirect" title="Alt Mariendorf (Berlin U-Bahn)">Alt Mariendorf</a> along the <a href="/wiki/U6_(Berlin_U-Bahn)" title="U6 (Berlin U-Bahn)">U6</a> via Rudow. The X11 bus continues to <a href="/wiki/Lichterfelde-West" class="mw-redirect" title="Lichterfelde-West">Lichterfelde-West</a> and to <a href="/wiki/Dahlem_(Berlin)" title="Dahlem (Berlin)">Dahlem</a>. There are also special express buses costing a surcharge dubbed "BER1" and "BER2" which connect the airport with <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Rathaus_Steglitz_station" title="Berlin Rathaus Steglitz station">Rathaus Steglitz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Potsdam_main_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Potsdam main station">Potsdam main station</a> respectively. Other bus lines also stop at a number of stations, providing connections with Berlin\'s public transport network and destinations in Brandenburg.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bicycle">Bicycle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Bicycle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The access to the airport by bicycle is considered lacking by the local <a href="/wiki/Allgemeiner_Deutscher_Fahrrad-Club" title="Allgemeiner Deutscher Fahrrad-Club">ADFC</a><sup id="cite_ref-385" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-385">&#91;385&#93;</a></sup> who demand a <a href="/wiki/Bicycle_highway" class="mw-redirect" title="Bicycle highway">bicycle highway</a> to the new airport. A reason cited for the lacking bicycle access is that the plans dating to 2006 made no such provision.<sup id="cite_ref-386" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-386">&#91;386&#93;</a></sup> The private website <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://bike2ber.de/">"Bike 2 BER"</a> explains the routes that do exist.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Commercial_and_exposition_area">Commercial and exposition area</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Commercial and exposition area">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span id="Berlin_Air_Show_.28ILA.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Berlin_Air_Show_(ILA)">Berlin Air Show (ILA)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Berlin Air Show (ILA)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg/220px-F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg/330px-F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg/440px-F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2800" data-file-height="1575" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:F-WWIQ_Airbus_A320_sharklet_ILA_2012_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A flight display performed by an <a href="/wiki/Airbus_A320-200" class="mw-redirect" title="Airbus A320-200">Airbus A320-200</a> at the Berlin Air Show</div></div></div>\n<p>On 3 July 2012, the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_ExpoCenter_Airport" title="Berlin ExpoCenter Airport">Berlin ExpoCenter Airport</a> opened on the southeastern portion of the airport grounds.<sup id="cite_ref-expocenter_387-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-expocenter-387">&#91;387&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Messe_Berlin" title="Messe Berlin">Messe Berlin</a> operates the 250,000 square metres (2,700,000&#160;sq&#160;ft) exposition facility that is primarily intended as the site of the biennial <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Air_Show" class="mw-redirect" title="Berlin Air Show">Berlin Air Show</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-bdli_388-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bdli-388">&#91;388&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Airport_Information_Centre">Airport Information Centre</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Airport Information Centre">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Coinciding with groundbreaking for construction of the new airport, an information and public relations centre called <i>airportworld</i> opened near the old Sch\xc3\xb6nefeld Airport. On 14 November 2007, the <i>Infotower</i>, a 32-metre-high (105&#160;ft) public viewing tower containing an exhibition about the new airport opened on the BER construction site.<sup id="cite_ref-BBI.Infotower_389-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBI.Infotower-389">&#91;389&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Business_park">Business park</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Business park">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The area surrounding BER is zoned as a commercial district. Plans call for the construction of shopping centres and parking structures as well as industrial, commercial and office spaces. Situated at the terminal complex will be the <i>BER Airport City</i> with an area of 16 hectares (40 acres). Marketing of the real estate began in autumn 2006 and beginning in 2009 offices, hotels, car rentals, four car parks with a capacity of 10,000, restaurants and retail spaces were built here.\n</p><p>To the north is the <i>BER Business Park Berlin</i> with a planned area of 109 hectares (270 acres) for industrial and commercial use as well as congress centers. A further <i>Business Park North</i> was proposed as a future use of the area of the old Sch\xc3\xb6nefeld terminal. However, those plans were put on hold due to the decision to incorporate the terminal into the new airport.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Controversies">Controversies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Controversies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>In September 2010, <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Flugsicherung" title="Deutsche Flugsicherung">Deutsche Flugsicherung</a> published aircraft arrival and departure routes for Berlin Brandenburg Airport which significantly differ from earlier ones used in the court decision for the construction permit. In the original maps, aircraft were expected to take off and land in a path parallel with the runway. The new plans saw flight paths that deviate from the runway direction by 15 degrees. Therefore, aircraft would now fly over areas in southern Berlin (<a href="/wiki/Lichtenrade" title="Lichtenrade">Lichtenrade</a>, <a href="/wiki/Steglitz" title="Steglitz">Steglitz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Zehlendorf,_Berlin" class="mw-redirect" title="Zehlendorf, Berlin">Zehlendorf</a>) and adjacent Brandenburg (<a href="/wiki/Teltow" title="Teltow">Teltow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stahnsdorf" title="Stahnsdorf">Stahnsdorf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kleinmachnow" title="Kleinmachnow">Kleinmachnow</a> and <a href="/wiki/Potsdam" title="Potsdam">Potsdam</a>) to the surprise of local residents. This prompted a wave of protests and a lawsuit that the courts rejected.<sup id="cite_ref-warner_390-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-warner-390">&#91;390&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Both the expansion of Sch\xc3\xb6nefeld Airport into BER and the quality of the connection to the railway network are the subject of public debate. The <i>B\xc3\xbcrgerverein Brandenburg-Berlin e.V.</i> represents local residents who protest an expansion of air traffic to and from the south of Berlin. Also, traffic and environmental experts criticise the late completion dates for the fast connection to the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Hauptbahnhof" title="Berlin Hauptbahnhof">Berlin Hauptbahnhof</a>. Still, Berlin Hauptbahnhof will be only a 30-minute journey with trains departing every 15 minutes upon inauguration. At the time of the originally planned opening date of BER, in 2011, this was expected to be reduced to 20 minutes after reconstruction of the Berlin section of the <a href="/wiki/Berlin%E2%80%93Dresden_railway" title="Berlin\xe2\x80\x93Dresden railway">Berlin\xe2\x80\x93Dresden railway</a>, which was planned to be finished by 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-dresdnerbahn_391-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dresdnerbahn-391">&#91;391&#93;</a></sup> However, delays in both the BER construction and the construction of the railway meant that the travel time will be 30 minutes until at least 2025.<sup id="cite_ref-392" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-392">&#91;392&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In May 2016, it emerged that a <a href="/wiki/Whistleblower" title="Whistleblower">whistle blower</a> on the airport project, who had alerted the public to major corruption within the project, had been poisoned with a "deadly substance" but survived after a three-month period of illness.<sup id="cite_ref-bbcpoison_393-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbcpoison-393">&#91;393&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Berlin_Brandenburg_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/List_of_airports_in_Germany" title="List of airports in Germany">List of airports in Germany</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_transport_megaprojects" title="List of transport megaprojects">List of transport megaprojects</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Megaproject" title="Megaproject">Megaproject</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Transport_in_Germany" title="Transport in Germany">Transport in Germany</a></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a
